User-specified model name\n    assigned_provider: Optional[str] = None   # User-specified provider\n    verify_cmd: Optional[str] = None\n    metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)\n```\n\nThe `PlannedStage` data class has two optional fields for storing user-specified model assignments:\n- `assigned_model`: The canonical model name (e.g., \"gpt-5.4-codex\", \"gemini-3.1-pro\")\n- `assigned_provider`: The provider string (e.g., \"codex\", \"google\", \"claude\")\n\n---\n\n## 2. **IntakeAgent.plan_task Accepts model_overrides** (harness/intake.py:87-109)\n\n```python\ndef plan_task(\n    self,\n    description: str,\n    *,\n    goal: str | None = None,\n    verify_cmd: str | None = None,\n    model_overrides: dict[str, tuple[str, str]] | None = None,  # stage_type -> (model, provider)\n) -> IntakeResult:\n    complexity = self.assess_complexity(description)\n    stage_defs = self.COMPLEXITY_RULES[complexity][\"stages\"]\n    overrides = model_overrides or {}\n    stages = [\n        PlannedStage(\n            stage_type=stage_type,\n            stage_order=index,\n            model_role=model_role,\n            assigned_model=overrides.get(stage_type, (None, None))[0],      # Extract model\n            assigned_provider=overrides.get(stage_type, (None, None))[1],   # provider_name)`\n- For each planned stage, looks up the override using the stage type\n- Populates `assigned_model` and `assigned_provider` fields from the override tuple\n- If no override exists for      model_role=planned.model_role,\n                assigned_model=planned.assigned_model,        # Persists user-specified model\n                assigned_provider=planned.assigned_provider,  # Creates `StageRecord` objects from `PlannedStage` instances\n- **Directly copies** `assigned_model` and `assigned_provider` to the database\n- Pre-assigned models are persisted in the SQLite database alongside stage metadata\n\n---\n\n## 4. **Harness._run_stage Skips QuotaRouter When Pre-Assigned** (harness/main.py:351-362)\n\n```python\nasync def _run_stage(self, task: TaskRecord, stage: StageRecord) -> None:\n    try:\n        if not stage.assigned_model or not stage.assigned_provider:\n            # Only invoke QuotaRouter if model NOT pre-assigned\n            choice = self.router.select_model(task, stage)\n            self.task_queue.assign_stage_model(\n                stage.stage_id,\n                choice.model,\n                choice.provider,\n                account_email=choice.account_email,\n                reason=choice.reason,\n            )\n            stage = self.task_queue.get_stage(stage.stage_id) or stage\n        \n        # Proceed with execution using assigned_model/assigned_provider\n        self._ensure_stage_runtime(stage)\n        previous = self.task_queue.list_completed_stages(task.task_id)\n        handoff_path = self.handoff.write_handoff(task, stage, previous)\n        # ... execution continues ...\n```\n\n**Key behavior:**\n- Line 353: Checks `if not stage.assigned_model or not stage.assigned_provider:`\n- If **both fields are set** (user pre-assigned), the `QuotaRouter.select_model()` call is **skipped entirely**\n- If **either field is missing** (no override), QuotaRouter selection is triggered\n- This allows user-specified models to bypass quota routing logic\n\n---\n\n## 5. **CLI --model-override Flag** (harness/main.py:547, 642-652)\n\n```python\n# Argument parser (line 547):\nsubmit.add_argument(\n    \"--model-override\",\n    action=\"append\",\n    default=[],\n    help=\"Override stage model (e.g. code=gemini-3.1-pro)\"\n)\n\n# CLI processing (lines 642-652):\nmodel_overrides = {}\nif getattr(args, \"model_override\", None):\n    registry = ModelRegistry()\n    for override in args.model_override:\n        if \"=\" in override:\n            stage, model_name = override.split(\"=\", 1)\n            stage = stage.strip()\n            model_name = model_name.strip()\n            canonical = registry.resolve(model_name)        # Normalize name\n            provider = registry.provider(model_name) or \"unknown\"\n            model_overrides[stage] = (canonical, provider)\n\ntask = harness.submit_task(\n    args.description,\n    title=args.title,\n    goal=args.goal,\n    verify_cmd=args.verify_cmd,\n    priority=args.priority,\n    working_dir=args.working_dir,\n    model_overrides=model_overrides if model_overrides else None,\n)\n```\n\n**CLI usage example:**\n```bash\npython -m harness.main submit \"Add feature X\" \\\n  --model-override code=gemini-3.1-pro \\\n  --model-override review=claude-opus-4-6 \\\n  --priority 80\n```\n\nThe CLI:\n- Accepts multiple `--model-override` flags\n- Each flag uses format: `stage_type=model_name`\n- Model names can be canonical or aliases (handled by ModelRegistry)\n- Builds a dict mapping stage types to (canonical_model, provider) tuples\n- Passes to `submit_task()` which propagates to `intake.plan_task()`\n\n---\n\n## 6. **ModelRegistry.resolve() Normalizes Model Names** (harness/model_registry.py:39-45, 104-127)\n\n```python\ndef resolve(self, name: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Resolve any name (canonical or alias) to its canonical name.\n    \n    Returns the input unchanged if it is not recognised — this keeps\n    the system open to ad-hoc model names that haven't been catalogued.\n    \"\"\"\n    return self._alias_to_canonical.get(name, name)\n\ndef _build_index(self) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Build alias → canonical mapping with collision detection.\"\"\"\n    for canonical, info in self._models.items():\n        self._register(canonical, canonical)\n        for alias in info.get(\"aliases\", []):\n            if alias and alias != canonical:\n                self._register(alias, canonical)\n\ndef provider(self, name: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Return the provider string for *name*.\"\"\"\n    canonical = self.resolve(name)\n    return self._models.get(canonical, {}).get(\"provider\", \"\")\n```\n\n**Model resolution workflow:**\n- Loads model catalog from `/home/ubuntu/scripts/code-orchestra/config/role_models.yaml`\n- Builds an alias index at initialization time\n- `resolve()` maps any name (canonical or alias) to canonical form\n- Unknown names are returned unchanged (allows ad-hoc model references)\n- `provider()` looks up provider after resolving to canonical name\n\n**Example from role_models.yaml:**\n```yaml\nmodels:\n  gpt-5.4-codex:\n    provider: codex\n    aliases: [codex, gpt-5.4, codex-balanced]\n  \n  claude-opus-4-6:\n    provider: claude\n    aliases: [opus, claude-opus]\n```\n\nUser can reference these models by any alias:\n- `gpt-5.4` → resolves to `gpt-5.4-codex` with provider `codex`\n- `opus` → resolves to `claude-opus-4-6` with provider `claude`\n\n---\n\n## 7. **StageExecutor Uses Assigned Models** (harness/stage_executor.py:71-90)\n\n```python\nasync def execute(self, stage: StageRecord, handoff_doc_path: str, working_dir: str | None) -> StageExecutionResult:\n    started_at = time.time()\n    prompt = Path(handoff_doc_path).read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    provider = stage.assigned_provider or self.chat_client.chat,\n            model=stage.assigned_model or \"\",      # Uses pre-assigned model\n            prompt=prompt,\n        )\n```\n\nThe `StageExecutor`:\n- Takes the pre-assigned (harness/models.py:34-42)\n\n```python\n@dataclass(slots=True)\nclass PlannedStage:\n    stage_type: str\n    stage_order: int\n    model_role: str\n    assigned_model: Optional[str] = None      # User-specified model name\n    assigned_provider: Optional[str] = None   # User-specified provider\n    verify_cmd: Optional[str] = None\n    metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)\n```\n\nThe `PlannedStage` data class has two optional fields for storing user-specified model assignments:\n- `assigned_model`: The canonical model name (e.g., \"gpt-5.4-codex\", \"gemini-3.1-pro\")\n- `assigned_provider`: The provider string (e.g., \"codex\", \"google\", \"claude\")\n\n---\n\n## 2. **IntakeAgent.plan_task Accepts model_overrides** (harness/intake.py:87-109)\n\n```python\ndef plan_task(\n    self,\n    description: str,\n    *,\n    goal: str | None = None,\n    verify_cmd: str | None = None,\n    model_overrides: dict[str, tuple[str, str]] | None = None,  # stage_type -> (model, provider)\n) -> IntakeResult:\n    complexity = self.assess_complexity(description)\n    stage_defs = self.COMPLEXITY_RULES[complexity][\"stages\"]\n    overrides = model_overrides or {}\n    stages = [\n        PlannedStage(\n            stage_type=stage_type,\n            stage_order=index,\n            model_role=model_role,\n            assigned_model=overrides.get(stage_type, (None, None))[0],      # Extract model\n            assigned_provider=overrides.get(stage_type, (None, None))[1],   # (stage_type, model_role) in enumerate(stage_defs, start=1)\n    ]\n```\n\nThe `IntakeAgent.plan_task` method:\n- Accepts `model_overrides` as a dict mapping `stage_type` to tuples of `(model_name, provider_name)`\n- For each planned stage, looks up the override using the stage type\n- Populates `assigned_model` and `assigned_provider` fields from the override tuple\n- If no override exists for a stage, leaves both fields as `None`\n\n---\n\n## 3. **TaskQueue.save_stages Persists Pre-Assignments** (harness/task_queue.py:139-197)\n\n```python\ndef save_stages(self, task_id: str, stages: Iterable[PlannedStage]) -> list[StageRecord]:\n    now = utcnow_iso()\n    records: list[StageRecord] = []\n    with self.db.connect() as conn:\n        for planned in stages:\n            record = StageRecord(\n                stage_id=uuid.uuid4().hex,\n                task_id=task_id,\n                stage_type=planned.stage_type,\n                stage_order=planned.stage_order,\n                model_role=planned.model_role,\n                assigned_model=planned.assigned_model,        # Persists user-specified model\n                assigned_provider=planned.assigned_provider,  # INSERT INTO stages (\n                    stage_id, task_id, stage_type, stage_order, model_role,\n                    assigned_model, assigned_provider, status, ...\n                ) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ...)\n                \"\"\",\n                (record.stage_id, ..., record.assigned_model, record.assigned_provider, ...),\n            )\n```\n\nThe `save_stages` method:\n- Creates `StageRecord` objects from `PlannedStage` instances\n- **Directly copies** `assigned_model` and `assigned_provider` to the database\n- Pre-assigned models are persisted in the SQLite database alongside stage metadata\n\n---\n\n## 4. **Harness._run_stage Skips QuotaRouter When Pre-Assigned** (harness/main.py:351-362)\n\n```python\nasync def _run_stage(self, task: TaskRecord, stage: StageRecord) -> None:\n    try:\n        if not stage.assigned_model or not stage.assigned_provider:\n            # Only invoke QuotaRouter if model NOT pre-assigned\n            choice = self.router.select_model(task, stage)\n            self.task_queue.assign_stage_model(\n                stage.stage_id,\n                choice.model,\n                choice.provider,\n                account_email=choice.account_email,\n                reason=choice.reason,\n            )\n            stage = self.task_queue.get_stage(stage.stage_id) or stage\n        \n        # Proceed with execution using assigned_model/assigned_provider\n        self._ensure_stage_runtime(stage)\n        previous = self.task_queue.list_completed_stages(task.task_id)\n        handoff_path = self.handoff.write_handoff(task, stage, previous)\n        # ... execution continues ...\n```\n\n**Key behavior:**\n- Line 353: Checks `if not stage.assigned_model or not stage.assigned_provider:`\n- If **both fields are set** (user pre-assigned), the `QuotaRouter.select_model()` call is **skipped entirely**\n- If **either field is missing** (no override), QuotaRouter selection is triggered\n- This allows user-specified models to bypass quota routing logic\n\n---\n\n## 5. **CLI --model-override Flag** (harness/main.py:547, 642-652)\n\n```python\n# Argument parser (line 547):\nsubmit.add_argument(\n    \"--model-override\",\n    action=\"append\",\n    default=[],\n    help=\"Override stage model (e.g. code=gemini-3.1-pro)\"\n)\n\n# CLI processing (lines 642-652):\nmodel_overrides = {}\nif getattr(args, \"model_override\", None):\n    registry = ModelRegistry()\n    for override in args.model_override:\n        if \"=\" in override:\n            stage, model_name = override.split(\"=\", 1)\n            stage = stage.strip()\n            model_name = model_name.strip()\n            canonical = registry.resolve(model_name)        # Normalize name\n            provider = registry.provider(model_name) or \"unknown\"\n            model_overrides[stage] = (canonical, provider)\n\ntask = harness.submit_task(\n    args.description,\n None,\n)\n```\n\n**CLI usage example:**\n```bash\npython -m harness.main submit \"Add feature X\" \\\n  --model-override code=gemini-3.1-pro \\\n  --model-override review=claude-opus-4-6 \\\n  --priority 80\n```\n\nThe CLI:\n- Accepts multiple `--model-override` flags\n- Each flag uses format: `stage_type=model_name`\n- Model names can be canonical or aliases (handled by ModelRegistry)\n- Builds a dict mapping stage types to (canonical_model, provider) tuples\n- Passes to `submit_task()` which propagates to `intake.plan_task()`\n\n---\n\n## 6. **ModelRegistry.resolve() Normalizes Model Names** (harness/model_registry.py:39-45, 104-127)\n\n```python\ndef resolve(self, name: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Resolve any name (canonical or alias) to its canonical name.\n    \n    Returns the input unchanged if it is not recognised — this keeps\n    the system open to ad-hoc model names that haven't been catalogued.\n    \"\"\"\n    return self._alias_to_canonical.get(name, name)\n\ndef _build_index(self) -> None:\n    \"\"\"Build alias → canonical mapping with collision detection.\"\"\"\n    for canonical, info in self._models.items():\n        self._register(canonical, canonical)\n        for alias in info.get(\"aliases\", []):\n            if alias and alias != canonical:\n                self._register(alias, canonical)\n\ndef provider(self, name: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Return the provider string for *name*.\"\"\"\n    canonical = self.resolve(name)\n    return self._models.get(canonical, {}).get(\"provider\", \"\")\n```\n\n**Model resolution workflow:**\n- Loads model catalog from `/home/ubuntu/scripts/code-orchestra/config/role_models.yaml`\n- Builds an alias index at initialization time\n- `resolve()` maps any name (canonical or alias) to canonical form\n- Unknown names are returned unchanged (allows ad-hoc model references)\n- `provider()` looks up provider after resolving to canonical name\n\n**Example from role_models.yaml:**\n```yaml\nmodels:\n  gpt-5.4-codex:\n    provider: codex\n    aliases: [codex, gpt-5.4, codex-balanced]\n  \n  claude-opus-4-6:\n    provider: claude\n    aliases: [opus, claude-opus]\n```\n\nUser can reference these models by any alias:\n- `gpt-5.4` → resolves to `gpt-5.4-codex` with provider `codex`\n- `opus` → resolves to `claude-opus-4-6` with provider
